e
 Silk Smita

 She had become a great tool to draw huge crowds at the box office
 tamil or telegu kii kai aisi filmein, jinamein nami hero hone ke baavjood koi unhen kharidne ko taiyaar na tha, unamem yadi silk kaa ek adad cabre dance daal diya jaataa, to vah haathon-haath bik jaataa tha

 According to a new research, the habit of chewing betel leaf can be instrumental in the war against a particular type of cancer
 bharat ke kuch sheersh shodh sansthaanon ke shodhakartaaon kaa daawa he ki paan ke pattey main ek khaas tarah kaa tatv paaya jaataa he jo jaanaleva chronic milwoid leukemia (siemail) se grast marijon kii cancerrodhi kshamta badha saktaa he
 Researchers at the Kolkata-based Institute of Hematology and Transition Medicine, Indian Institute of Chemical Biology (IICB) and Piramal Life Sciences, Mumbai have concluded that betel leaves are anticancer
 iaisibi main department of cancer biology and inlemetary dysorders ke santu bandyopadhyaay ne ieenes se baatcheet karte hue kaha, 'paan ke patton se praapt maadak tatv kaa ek bada sanghatak he hydroxicevikol (echsiech) jo leukemia rodhi he
 The research findings are based on an in-depth report published in 2011 in a prestigious journal called Frontiers in Bioscience (elite Edition)
 jaapnij cancer association ke is aadhikarik jarnal main chhapi adhyayan report ko in shodhakartaaon ne behad vishwasaneey qaraar diya he
 According to researchers, HCH not only kills cancerous CML cells, but also destroys cancer cells that have developed immunity to drugs
 yah tatv insaan kii pratirodhi kshamta ke liye behad mahatvapurn maane jane vaale peripheral blad monocuclear cells (pibiemasi) ko kam se kam nuksaan pahunchaate hue cancer koshikaon ko nasht karata he
 It is noteworthy that leukemia is mainly a disease of adults, about 100,000 cases of which come to light in India every year
 rakt or asthi majja kii yah jaanaleva beemaari amuman adhedavastha main jakadti he
 In the person suffering from this disease, the rate of formation of white blood cells increases abnormally and normal medicines do not affect the body
 har saal hajaaron log isse marate hai
 a drug called imatinib is very effective in treating this disease, but this drug stops working due to the creation of a mutation process called T3151 in the body
 koi bhi aisi dawa philhal maujuud nahin he jo is avarohak muteshan yaa sankriya ko ghatit hone se roak sake
 According to new research, the HCH present in betel leaf induces cancer cells that have become resistant to drugs to undergo the auto-fission process known as apoptosis

 The ministry said that North Korea's top leader Kim is responsible for human rights abuses in his role as the country's head of home security and public security affairs
 washington main adhikariyon ke anusaar, 'uttar korea ke grih suraksha mantralay ne raajnneetik kaidi shiviron main 80 hajaar se lekar 120,000 kaidiyon ko rakhaa, unhen maut kii sajaa di, yon pratadna di, bhukhe maaraa or unase gulaamon kii tarah kaam karavaaya janaa aam baat rahi he
 The US has said that the Ministry of Public Security, which operates under Kim's supervision, runs a network of police stations, detention centers and labor camps where suspects are kept for questioning and tortured
 ' For the first time, the US administration has identified other top leaders directly involved in human rights, including Public Safety Minister Choi Pu Il, a senior official of the same ministry, Ri Song Chul, and bureau director Kang Song with the Ministry of Home Security Are included
